  4 32 The amendment provides that a person elected as governor,
  4 33 lieutenant governor, secretary of state, auditor of state,
  4 34 treasurer of state, or attorney general shall not serve more
  4 35 than three consecutive terms in that respective office. The
  5  1 amendment also provides that if the general assembly provides
  5  2 for the election of a state executive officer, that the officer
  5  3 shall not serve more than 12 consecutive years in that office.
  5  4    The amendment provides that if a person is elected,
  5  5 elevated, or appointed as applicable, to serve a portion of
  5  6 a term in these respective offices, the term shall not be
  5  7 included in counting terms of service if the person did not
  5  8 serve at least one=half of the full term. The amendment
  5  9 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 10 2021.
  5 11    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  5 12 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  5 13 electorate for ratification.
       LSB 5488XS (3) 86
       aw/sc
  2  4    3.  Section 6 of Article IV of the Constitution of the State
  2  5 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  2  6 Eligibility.SEC. 6.  No person shall be eligible to the
  2  7 office of governor, or lieutenant governor, who shall not have
  2  8 been a citizen of the United States, and a resident of the
  2  9 state, two years next preceding the election, and attained the
  2 10 age of thirty years at the time of said election.
  2 11    A person shall not be elected for a term as governor if
  2 12 the term would result in the person serving more than a total
  2 13 of three consecutive terms as governor.  A person shall not
  2 14 be elected for a term as lieutenant governor if the term
  2 15 would result in the person serving more than a total of three
  2 16 consecutive terms as lieutenant governor.  If a person is
  2 17 elevated or appointed to serve a portion of a term to which
  2 18 some other person was elected but that person died in office
  2 19 or resigned from office or was  otherwise removed from office,
  2 20 that portion of a term served shall not be included in the
  2 21 terms of service for purposes of this limitation if the person
  2 22 did not serve for at least one=half of the four=year term.
  2 23 This limitation on terms of service applies to terms of office
  2 24 beginning on or after January 1, 2021.
  2 25    4.  Section 22 of Article IV of the Constitution of the State
  2 26 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  2 27 Secretary ==== auditor ==== treasurer.SEC. 22.  A secretary of
  2 28 state, an auditor of state, and a treasurer of state shall be
  2 29 elected by the qualified electors at the same time that the
  2 30 governor is elected and for a four=year term commencing on the
  2 31 first day of January next after their election, and they shall
  2 32 perform such duties as may be provided by law.
  2 33    A person shall not be elected for a term as secretary of
  2 34 state if the term would result in the person serving more
  2 35 than a total of three consecutive terms in that office. A
  3  1 person shall not be elected for a term as auditor of state
  3  2 if the term would result in the person serving more than a
  3  3 total of three consecutive terms in that office. A person
  3  4 shall not be elected for a term as treasurer of state if the
  3  5 term would result in the person serving more than a total of
  3  6 three consecutive terms in that office. If a person appointed
  3  7 to serve a portion of a term to which some other person was
  3  8 elected, but that person died in office or resigned from office
  3  9 or was otherwise removed from office, that portion of a term
  3 10 served shall not be included in the terms of service for
  3 11 purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for at
  3 12 least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on terms
  3 13 of service applies to terms of office beginning on or after
  3 14 January 1, 2021.
  3 15    5.  The Constitution of the State of Iowa is amended by
  3 16 adding the following new section to Article IV:
  3 17 Elected state executive officer ==== term limits.SEC. 23.  If
  3 18 the general assembly provides by law for the election of a
  3 19 state executive officer by the people, a person shall not be
  3 20 elected for a term to that office if the term would result in
  3 21 the person serving more than a total of twelve years in that
  3 22 office. If a person appointed to serve a portion of a term to
  3 23 which some other person was elected, but that person died in
  3 24 office or resigned from office or was otherwise removed from
  3 25 office, that portion of a term served shall not be included
  3 26 in the terms of service for purposes of this limitation if
  3 27 the person did not serve for at least one=half of the term of
  3 28 office. This limitation on terms of service applies to terms
  3 29 of office beginning on or after January 1, 2021.
  3 30    6.  Section 12 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  3 31 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  3 32 Attorney general.SEC. 12.  The general assembly shall
  3 33 provide, by law, for the election of an attorney general by the
  3 34 people, whose term of office shall be four years, and until his
  3 35 successor is elected and qualifies.
  4  1 A person shall not be elected for a term as attorney general
  4  2 if the term would result in the person serving more than a
  4  3 total of three consecutive terms in that office. If a person
  4  4 appointed to serve a portion of a term to which some other
  4  5 person was elected, but that person died in office or resigned
  4  6 from office or was otherwise removed from office, that portion
  4  7 of a term served shall not be included in the terms of service
  4  8 for purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for
  4  9 at least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on
  4 10 terms of service applies to terms of office beginning on or
  4 11 after January 1, 2021.
  4 12    Sec. 2.  REFERRAL AND PUBLICATION.  The foregoing amendment
  4 13 to the Constitution of the State of Iowa is referred to the
  4 14 general assembly to be chosen at the next general election
  4 15 for members of the general assembly, and the secretary of
  4 16 state is directed to cause the same to be published for three
  4 17 consecutive months previous to the date of that election as
  4 18 provided by law.
  4 19                           EXPLANATION
  4 20 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  4 21 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  4 22    This joint resolution proposes an amendment to the
  4 23 Constitution of the State of Iowa limiting terms of service
  4 24 for persons elected to the offices of representative or
  4 25 senator in the general assembly, governor, lieutenant governor,
  4 26 secretary of state, auditor of state, treasurer of state,
  4 27 attorney general, and any other elected state executive
  4 28 officer.  The amendment provides that a member of the house
  4 29 of representatives shall not serve more than six consecutive
  4 30 terms as a representative, and that a member of the senate
  4 31 shall not serve more than three consecutive terms as a senator.
  4 32 The amendment provides that a person elected as governor,
  4 33 lieutenant governor, secretary of state, auditor of state,
  4 34 treasurer of state, or attorney general shall not serve more
  4 35 than three consecutive terms in that respective office. The
  5  1 amendment also provides that if the general assembly provides
  5  2 for the election of a state executive officer, that the officer
  5  3 shall not serve more than 12 consecutive years in that office.
  5  4    The amendment provides that if a person is elected,
  5  5 elevated, or appointed as applicable, to serve a portion of
  5  6 a term in these respective offices, the term shall not be
  5  7 included in counting terms of service if the person did not
  5  8 serve at least one=half of the full term. The amendment
  5  9 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 10 2021.
  5 11    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  5 12 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  5 13 electorate for ratification.

  2 16 consecutive terms as lieutenant governor.  If a person is
  2 17 elevated or appointed to serve a portion of a term to which
  2 18 some other person was elected but that person died in office
  2 19 or resigned from office or was  otherwise removed from office,
  2 20 that portion of a term served shall not be included in the
  2 21 terms of service for purposes of this limitation if the person
  2 22 did not serve for at least one=half of the four=year term.
  2 23 This limitation on terms of service applies to terms of office
  2 24 beginning on or after January 1, 2021.
  2 25    4.  Section 22 of Article IV of the Constitution of the State
  2 26 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  2 27 Secretary ==== auditor ==== treasurer.SEC. 22.  A secretary of
  2 28 state, an auditor of state, and a treasurer of state shall be
  2 29 elected by the qualified electors at the same time that the
  2 30 governor is elected and for a four=year term commencing on the
  2 31 first day of January next after their election, and they shall
  2 32 perform such duties as may be provided by law.
  2 33    A person shall not be elected for a term as secretary of
  2 34 state if the term would result in the person serving more
  2 35 than a total of three consecutive terms in that office. A
  3  1 person shall not be elected for a term as auditor of state
  3  2 if the term would result in the person serving more than a
  3  3 total of three consecutive terms in that office. A person
  3  4 shall not be elected for a term as treasurer of state if the
  3  5 term would result in the person serving more than a total of
  3  6 three consecutive terms in that office. If a person appointed
  3  7 to serve a portion of a term to which some other person was
  3  8 elected, but that person died in office or resigned from office
  3  9 or was otherwise removed from office, that portion of a term
  3 10 served shall not be included in the terms of service for
  3 11 purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for at
  3 12 least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on terms
  3 13 of service applies to terms of office beginning on or after
  3 14 January 1, 2021.
  3 15    5.  The Constitution of the State of Iowa is amended by
  3 16 adding the following new section to Article IV:
  3 17 Elected state executive officer ==== term limits.SEC. 23.  If
  3 18 the general assembly provides by law for the election of a
  3 19 state executive officer by the people, a person shall not be
  3 20 elected for a term to that office if the term would result in
  3 21 the person serving more than a total of twelve years in that
  3 22 office. If a person appointed to serve a portion of a term to
  3 23 which some other person was elected, but that person died in
  3 24 office or resigned from office or was otherwise removed from
  3 25 office, that portion of a term served shall not be included
  3 26 in the terms of service for purposes of this limitation if
  3 27 the person did not serve for at least one=half of the term of
  3 28 office. This limitation on terms of service applies to terms
  3 29 of office beginning on or after January 1, 2021.
  3 30    6.  Section 12 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  3 31 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  3 32 Attorney general.SEC. 12.  The general assembly shall
  3 33 provide, by law, for the election of an attorney general by the
  3 34 people, whose term of office shall be four years, and until his
  3 35 successor is elected and qualifies.
  4  1 A person shall not be elected for a term as attorney general
  4  2 if the term would result in the person serving more than a
  4  3 total of three consecutive terms in that office. If a person
  4  4 appointed to serve a portion of a term to which some other
  4  5 person was elected, but that person died in office or resigned
  4  6 from office or was otherwise removed from office, that portion
  4  7 of a term served shall not be included in the terms of service
  4  8 for purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for
  4  9 at least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on
  4 10 terms of service applies to terms of office beginning on or
  4 11 after January 1, 2021.
  4 12    Sec. 2.  REFERRAL AND PUBLICATION.  The foregoing amendment
  4 13 to the Constitution of the State of Iowa is referred to the
  4 14 general assembly to be chosen at the next general election
  4 15 for members of the general assembly, and the secretary of
  4 16 state is directed to cause the same to be published for three
  4 17 consecutive months previous to the date of that election as
  4 18 provided by law.
  4 19                           EXPLANATION
  4 20 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  4 21 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  4 22    This joint resolution proposes an amendment to the
  4 23 Constitution of the State of Iowa limiting terms of service
  4 24 for persons elected to the offices of representative or
  4 25 senator in the general assembly, governor, lieutenant governor,
  4 26 secretary of state, auditor of state, treasurer of state,
  4 27 attorney general, and any other elected state executive
  4 28 officer.  The amendment provides that a member of the house
  4 29 of representatives shall not serve more than six consecutive
  4 30 terms as a representative, and that a member of the senate
  4 31 shall not serve more than three consecutive terms as a senator.
  4 32 The amendment provides that a person elected as governor,
  4 33 lieutenant governor, secretary of state, auditor of state,
  4 34 treasurer of state, or attorney general shall not serve more
  4 35 than three consecutive terms in that respective office. The
  5  1 amendment also provides that if the general assembly provides
  5  2 for the election of a state executive officer, that the officer
  5  3 shall not serve more than 12 consecutive years in that office.
  5  4    The amendment provides that if a person is elected,
  5  5 elevated, or appointed as applicable, to serve a portion of
  5  6 a term in these respective offices, the term shall not be
  5  7 included in counting terms of service if the person did not
  5  8 serve at least one=half of the full term. The amendment
  5  9 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 10 2021.
  5 11    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  5 12 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  5 13 electorate for ratification.

  2 13 of three consecutive terms as governor.  A person shall not
  2 14 be elected for a term as lieutenant governor if the term
  2 15 would result in the person serving more than a total of three
  2 16 consecutive terms as lieutenant governor.  If a person is
  2 17 elevated or appointed to serve a portion of a term to which
  2 18 some other person was elected but that person died in office

  3 27 the person did not serve for at least one=half of the term of
  3 28 office. This limitation on terms of service applies to terms
  3 29 of office beginning on or after January 1, 2021.
  3 30    6.  Section 12 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  3 31 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  3 32 Attorney general.SEC. 12.  The general assembly shall
  3 33 provide, by law, for the election of an attorney general by the
  3 34 people, whose term of office shall be four years, and until his
  3 35 successor is elected and qualifies.
  4  1 A person shall not be elected for a term as attorney general
  4  2 if the term would result in the person serving more than a
  4  3 total of three consecutive terms in that office. If a person
  4  4 appointed to serve a portion of a term to which some other
  4  5 person was elected, but that person died in office or resigned
  4  6 from office or was otherwise removed from office, that portion
  4  7 of a term served shall not be included in the terms of service
  4  8 for purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for
  4  9 at least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on
  4 10 terms of service applies to terms of office beginning on or
  4 11 after January 1, 2021.
  4 12    Sec. 2.  REFERRAL AND PUBLICATION.  The foregoing amendment
  4 13 to the Constitution of the State of Iowa is referred to the
  4 14 general assembly to be chosen at the next general election
  4 15 for members of the general assembly, and the secretary of
  4 16 state is directed to cause the same to be published for three
  4 17 consecutive months previous to the date of that election as
  4 18 provided by law.
  4 19                           EXPLANATION
  4 20 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  4 21 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  4 22    This joint resolution proposes an amendment to the
  4 23 Constitution of the State of Iowa limiting terms of service
  4 24 for persons elected to the offices of representative or
  4 25 senator in the general assembly, governor, lieutenant governor,
  4 26 secretary of state, auditor of state, treasurer of state,
  4 27 attorney general, and any other elected state executive
  4 28 officer.  The amendment provides that a member of the house
  4 29 of representatives shall not serve more than six consecutive
  4 30 terms as a representative, and that a member of the senate
  4 31 shall not serve more than three consecutive terms as a senator.
  4 32 The amendment provides that a person elected as governor,
  4 33 lieutenant governor, secretary of state, auditor of state,
  4 34 treasurer of state, or attorney general shall not serve more
  4 35 than three consecutive terms in that respective office. The
  5  1 amendment also provides that if the general assembly provides
  5  2 for the election of a state executive officer, that the officer
  5  3 shall not serve more than 12 consecutive years in that office.
  5  4    The amendment provides that if a person is elected,
  5  5 elevated, or appointed as applicable, to serve a portion of
  5  6 a term in these respective offices, the term shall not be
  5  7 included in counting terms of service if the person did not
  5  8 serve at least one=half of the full term. The amendment
  5  9 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 10 2021.
  5 11    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  5 12 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  5 13 electorate for ratification.

  2 17 elevated or appointed to serve a portion of a term to which

  2 20 that portion of a term served shall not be included in the
  2 21 terms of service for purposes of this limitation if the person

  2 23 This limitation on terms of service applies to terms of office

  2 30 governor is elected and for a four=year term commencing on the

  3 16 adding the following new section to Article IV:
  3 17 Elected state executive officer ==== term limits.SEC. 23.  If
  3 18 the general assembly provides by law for the election of a
  3 19 state executive officer by the people, a person shall not be
  3 20 elected for a term to that office if the term would result in
  3 21 the person serving more than a total of twelve years in that
  3 22 office. If a person appointed to serve a portion of a term to
  3 23 which some other person was elected, but that person died in
  3 24 office or resigned from office or was otherwise removed from
  3 25 office, that portion of a term served shall not be included
  3 26 in the terms of service for purposes of this limitation if
  3 27 the person did not serve for at least one=half of the term of
  3 28 office. This limitation on terms of service applies to terms
  3 29 of office beginning on or after January 1, 2021.

  2 24 beginning on or after January 1, 2021.
  2 25    4.  Section 22 of Article IV of the Constitution of the State
  2 26 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  2 27 Secretary ==== auditor ==== treasurer.SEC. 22.  A secretary of
  2 28 state, an auditor of state, and a treasurer of state shall be
  2 29 elected by the qualified electors at the same time that the
  2 30 governor is elected and for a four=year term commencing on the
  2 31 first day of January next after their election, and they shall
  2 32 perform such duties as may be provided by law.
  2 33    A person shall not be elected for a term as secretary of
  2 34 state if the term would result in the person serving more
  2 35 than a total of three consecutive terms in that office. A
  3  1 person shall not be elected for a term as auditor of state
  3  2 if the term would result in the person serving more than a
  3  3 total of three consecutive terms in that office. A person
  3  4 shall not be elected for a term as treasurer of state if the
  3  5 term would result in the person serving more than a total of
  3  6 three consecutive terms in that office. If a person appointed
  3  7 to serve a portion of a term to which some other person was
  3  8 elected, but that person died in office or resigned from office
  3  9 or was otherwise removed from office, that portion of a term
  3 10 served shall not be included in the terms of service for
  3 11 purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for at
  3 12 least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on terms
  3 13 of service applies to terms of office beginning on or after
  3 14 January 1, 2021.
  3 15    5.  The Constitution of the State of Iowa is amended by
  3 16 adding the following new section to Article IV:
  3 17 Elected state executive officer ==== term limits.SEC. 23.  If
  3 18 the general assembly provides by law for the election of a
  3 19 state executive officer by the people, a person shall not be
  3 20 elected for a term to that office if the term would result in
  3 21 the person serving more than a total of twelve years in that
  3 22 office. If a person appointed to serve a portion of a term to
  3 23 which some other person was elected, but that person died in
  3 24 office or resigned from office or was otherwise removed from
  3 25 office, that portion of a term served shall not be included
  3 26 in the terms of service for purposes of this limitation if
  3 27 the person did not serve for at least one=half of the term of
  3 28 office. This limitation on terms of service applies to terms
  3 29 of office beginning on or after January 1, 2021.
  3 30    6.  Section 12 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  3 31 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  3 32 Attorney general.SEC. 12.  The general assembly shall
  3 33 provide, by law, for the election of an attorney general by the
  3 34 people, whose term of office shall be four years, and until his
  3 35 successor is elected and qualifies.
  4  1 A person shall not be elected for a term as attorney general
  4  2 if the term would result in the person serving more than a
  4  3 total of three consecutive terms in that office. If a person
  4  4 appointed to serve a portion of a term to which some other
  4  5 person was elected, but that person died in office or resigned
  4  6 from office or was otherwise removed from office, that portion
  4  7 of a term served shall not be included in the terms of service
  4  8 for purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for
  4  9 at least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on
  4 10 terms of service applies to terms of office beginning on or
  4 11 after January 1, 2021.
  4 12    Sec. 2.  REFERRAL AND PUBLICATION.  The foregoing amendment
  4 13 to the Constitution of the State of Iowa is referred to the
  4 14 general assembly to be chosen at the next general election
  4 15 for members of the general assembly, and the secretary of
  4 16 state is directed to cause the same to be published for three
  4 17 consecutive months previous to the date of that election as
  4 18 provided by law.
  4 19                           EXPLANATION
  4 20 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  4 21 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  4 22    This joint resolution proposes an amendment to the
  4 23 Constitution of the State of Iowa limiting terms of service
  4 24 for persons elected to the offices of representative or
  4 25 senator in the general assembly, governor, lieutenant governor,
  4 26 secretary of state, auditor of state, treasurer of state,
  4 27 attorney general, and any other elected state executive
  4 28 officer.  The amendment provides that a member of the house
  4 29 of representatives shall not serve more than six consecutive
  4 30 terms as a representative, and that a member of the senate
  4 31 shall not serve more than three consecutive terms as a senator.
  4 32 The amendment provides that a person elected as governor,
  4 33 lieutenant governor, secretary of state, auditor of state,
  4 34 treasurer of state, or attorney general shall not serve more
  4 35 than three consecutive terms in that respective office. The
  5  1 amendment also provides that if the general assembly provides
  5  2 for the election of a state executive officer, that the officer
  5  3 shall not serve more than 12 consecutive years in that office.
  5  4    The amendment provides that if a person is elected,
  5  5 elevated, or appointed as applicable, to serve a portion of
  5  6 a term in these respective offices, the term shall not be
  5  7 included in counting terms of service if the person did not
  5  8 serve at least one=half of the full term. The amendment
  5  9 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 10 2021.
  5 11    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  5 12 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  5 13 electorate for ratification.

  5  2 for the election of a state executive officer, that the officer
  5  3 shall not serve more than 12 consecutive years in that office.
  5  4    The amendment provides that if a person is elected,
  5  5 elevated, or appointed as applicable, to serve a portion of
  5  6 a term in these respective offices, the term shall not be
  5  7 included in counting terms of service if the person did not
  5  8 serve at least one=half of the full term. The amendment
  5  9 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 10 2021.
  5 11    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  5 12 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  5 13 electorate for ratification.
       LSB 5488XS (3) 86
       aw/sc
  2 22 did not serve for at least one=half of the four=year term.
  2 23 This limitation on terms of service applies to terms of office
  2 24 beginning on or after January 1, 2021.
  2 25    4.  Section 22 of Article IV of the Constitution of the State
  2 26 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  2 27 Secretary ==== auditor ==== treasurer.SEC. 22.  A secretary of
  2 28 state, an auditor of state, and a treasurer of state shall be
  2 29 elected by the qualified electors at the same time that the
  2 30 governor is elected and for a four=year term commencing on the
  2 31 first day of January next after their election, and they shall
  2 32 perform such duties as may be provided by law.
  2 33    A person shall not be elected for a term as secretary of
  2 34 state if the term would result in the person serving more
  2 35 than a total of three consecutive terms in that office. A
  3  1 person shall not be elected for a term as auditor of state
  3  2 if the term would result in the person serving more than a
  3  3 total of three consecutive terms in that office. A person
  3  4 shall not be elected for a term as treasurer of state if the
  3  5 term would result in the person serving more than a total of
  3  6 three consecutive terms in that office. If a person appointed
  3  7 to serve a portion of a term to which some other person was
  3  8 elected, but that person died in office or resigned from office
  3  9 or was otherwise removed from office, that portion of a term
  3 10 served shall not be included in the terms of service for
  3 11 purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for at
  3 12 least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on terms
  3 13 of service applies to terms of office beginning on or after
  3 14 January 1, 2021.
  3 15    5.  The Constitution of the State of Iowa is amended by
  3 16 adding the following new section to Article IV:
  3 17 Elected state executive officer ==== term limits.SEC. 23.  If
  3 18 the general assembly provides by law for the election of a
  3 19 state executive officer by the people, a person shall not be
  3 20 elected for a term to that office if the term would result in
  3 21 the person serving more than a total of twelve years in that
  3 22 office. If a person appointed to serve a portion of a term to
  3 23 which some other person was elected, but that person died in
  3 24 office or resigned from office or was otherwise removed from
  3 25 office, that portion of a term served shall not be included
  3 26 in the terms of service for purposes of this limitation if
  3 27 the person did not serve for at least one=half of the term of
  3 28 office. This limitation on terms of service applies to terms
  3 29 of office beginning on or after January 1, 2021.
  3 30    6.  Section 12 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  3 31 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  3 32 Attorney general.SEC. 12.  The general assembly shall
  3 33 provide, by law, for the election of an attorney general by the
  3 34 people, whose term of office shall be four years, and until his
  3 35 successor is elected and qualifies.
  4  1 A person shall not be elected for a term as attorney general
  4  2 if the term would result in the person serving more than a
  4  3 total of three consecutive terms in that office. If a person
  4  4 appointed to serve a portion of a term to which some other
  4  5 person was elected, but that person died in office or resigned
  4  6 from office or was otherwise removed from office, that portion
  4  7 of a term served shall not be included in the terms of service
  4  8 for purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for
  4  9 at least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on
  4 10 terms of service applies to terms of office beginning on or
  4 11 after January 1, 2021.
  4 12    Sec. 2.  REFERRAL AND PUBLICATION.  The foregoing amendment
  4 13 to the Constitution of the State of Iowa is referred to the
  4 14 general assembly to be chosen at the next general election
  4 15 for members of the general assembly, and the secretary of
  4 16 state is directed to cause the same to be published for three
  4 17 consecutive months previous to the date of that election as
  4 18 provided by law.
  4 19                           EXPLANATION
  4 20 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  4 21 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  4 22    This joint resolution proposes an amendment to the
  4 23 Constitution of the State of Iowa limiting terms of service
  4 24 for persons elected to the offices of representative or
  4 25 senator in the general assembly, governor, lieutenant governor,
  4 26 secretary of state, auditor of state, treasurer of state,
  4 27 attorney general, and any other elected state executive
  4 28 officer.  The amendment provides that a member of the house
  4 29 of representatives shall not serve more than six consecutive
  4 30 terms as a representative, and that a member of the senate
  4 31 shall not serve more than three consecutive terms as a senator.
  4 32 The amendment provides that a person elected as governor,
  4 33 lieutenant governor, secretary of state, auditor of state,
  4 34 treasurer of state, or attorney general shall not serve more
  4 35 than three consecutive terms in that respective office. The
  5  1 amendment also provides that if the general assembly provides
  5  2 for the election of a state executive officer, that the officer
  5  3 shall not serve more than 12 consecutive years in that office.
  5  4    The amendment provides that if a person is elected,
  5  5 elevated, or appointed as applicable, to serve a portion of
  5  6 a term in these respective offices, the term shall not be
  5  7 included in counting terms of service if the person did not
  5  8 serve at least one=half of the full term. The amendment
  5  9 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 10 2021.
  5 11    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  5 12 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  5 13 electorate for ratification.

  5  8 serve at least one=half of the full term. The amendment
  5  9 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 10 2021.
  5 11    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  5 12 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  5 13 electorate for ratification.
       LSB 5488XS (3) 86
       aw/sc
  2 27 Secretary ==== auditor ==== treasurer.SEC. 22.  A secretary of
  2 28 state, an auditor of state, and a treasurer of state shall be
  2 29 elected by the qualified electors at the same time that the
  2 30 governor is elected and for a four=year term commencing on the
  2 31 first day of January next after their election, and they shall
  2 32 perform such duties as may be provided by law.
  2 33    A person shall not be elected for a term as secretary of
  2 34 state if the term would result in the person serving more
  2 35 than a total of three consecutive terms in that office. A
  3  1 person shall not be elected for a term as auditor of state
  3  2 if the term would result in the person serving more than a
  3  3 total of three consecutive terms in that office. A person
  3  4 shall not be elected for a term as treasurer of state if the
  3  5 term would result in the person serving more than a total of
  3  6 three consecutive terms in that office. If a person appointed
  3  7 to serve a portion of a term to which some other person was
  3  8 elected, but that person died in office or resigned from office
  3  9 or was otherwise removed from office, that portion of a term
  3 10 served shall not be included in the terms of service for
  3 11 purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for at
  3 12 least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on terms
  3 13 of service applies to terms of office beginning on or after
  3 14 January 1, 2021.
  3 15    5.  The Constitution of the State of Iowa is amended by
  3 16 adding the following new section to Article IV:
  3 17 Elected state executive officer ==== term limits.SEC. 23.  If
  3 18 the general assembly provides by law for the election of a
  3 19 state executive officer by the people, a person shall not be
  3 20 elected for a term to that office if the term would result in
  3 21 the person serving more than a total of twelve years in that
  3 22 office. If a person appointed to serve a portion of a term to
  3 23 which some other person was elected, but that person died in
  3 24 office or resigned from office or was otherwise removed from
  3 25 office, that portion of a term served shall not be included
  3 26 in the terms of service for purposes of this limitation if
  3 27 the person did not serve for at least one=half of the term of
  3 28 office. This limitation on terms of service applies to terms
  3 29 of office beginning on or after January 1, 2021.
  3 30    6.  Section 12 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  3 31 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  3 32 Attorney general.SEC. 12.  The general assembly shall
  3 33 provide, by law, for the election of an attorney general by the
  3 34 people, whose term of office shall be four years, and until his
  3 35 successor is elected and qualifies.
  4  1 A person shall not be elected for a term as attorney general
  4  2 if the term would result in the person serving more than a
  4  3 total of three consecutive terms in that office. If a person
  4  4 appointed to serve a portion of a term to which some other
  4  5 person was elected, but that person died in office or resigned
  4  6 from office or was otherwise removed from office, that portion
  4  7 of a term served shall not be included in the terms of service
  4  8 for purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for
  4  9 at least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on
  4 10 terms of service applies to terms of office beginning on or
  4 11 after January 1, 2021.
  4 12    Sec. 2.  REFERRAL AND PUBLICATION.  The foregoing amendment
  4 13 to the Constitution of the State of Iowa is referred to the
  4 14 general assembly to be chosen at the next general election
  4 15 for members of the general assembly, and the secretary of
  4 16 state is directed to cause the same to be published for three
  4 17 consecutive months previous to the date of that election as
  4 18 provided by law.
  4 19                           EXPLANATION
  4 20 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  4 21 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  4 22    This joint resolution proposes an amendment to the
  4 23 Constitution of the State of Iowa limiting terms of service
  4 24 for persons elected to the offices of representative or
  4 25 senator in the general assembly, governor, lieutenant governor,
  4 26 secretary of state, auditor of state, treasurer of state,
  4 27 attorney general, and any other elected state executive
  4 28 officer.  The amendment provides that a member of the house
  4 29 of representatives shall not serve more than six consecutive
  4 30 terms as a representative, and that a member of the senate
  4 31 shall not serve more than three consecutive terms as a senator.
  4 32 The amendment provides that a person elected as governor,
  4 33 lieutenant governor, secretary of state, auditor of state,
  4 34 treasurer of state, or attorney general shall not serve more
  4 35 than three consecutive terms in that respective office. The
  5  1 amendment also provides that if the general assembly provides
  5  2 for the election of a state executive officer, that the officer
  5  3 shall not serve more than 12 consecutive years in that office.
  5  4    The amendment provides that if a person is elected,
  5  5 elevated, or appointed as applicable, to serve a portion of
  5  6 a term in these respective offices, the term shall not be
  5  7 included in counting terms of service if the person did not
  5  8 serve at least one=half of the full term. The amendment
  5  9 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 10 2021.
  5 11    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  5 12 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  5 13 electorate for ratification.

  3 24 office or resigned from office or was otherwise removed from
  3 25 office, that portion of a term served shall not be included
  3 26 in the terms of service for purposes of this limitation if
  3 27 the person did not serve for at least one=half of the term of
  3 28 office. This limitation on terms of service applies to terms
  3 29 of office beginning on or after January 1, 2021.
  3 30    6.  Section 12 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  3 31 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  3 32 Attorney general.SEC. 12.  The general assembly shall
  3 33 provide, by law, for the election of an attorney general by the
  3 34 people, whose term of office shall be four years, and until his
  3 35 successor is elected and qualifies.
  4  1 A person shall not be elected for a term as attorney general
  4  2 if the term would result in the person serving more than a
  4  3 total of three consecutive terms in that office. If a person
  4  4 appointed to serve a portion of a term to which some other
  4  5 person was elected, but that person died in office or resigned
  4  6 from office or was otherwise removed from office, that portion
  4  7 of a term served shall not be included in the terms of service
  4  8 for purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for
  4  9 at least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on
  4 10 terms of service applies to terms of office beginning on or
  4 11 after January 1, 2021.
  4 12    Sec. 2.  REFERRAL AND PUBLICATION.  The foregoing amendment
  4 13 to the Constitution of the State of Iowa is referred to the
  4 14 general assembly to be chosen at the next general election
  4 15 for members of the general assembly, and the secretary of
  4 16 state is directed to cause the same to be published for three
  4 17 consecutive months previous to the date of that election as
  4 18 provided by law.
  4 19                           EXPLANATION
  4 20 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  4 21 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  4 22    This joint resolution proposes an amendment to the
  4 23 Constitution of the State of Iowa limiting terms of service
  4 24 for persons elected to the offices of representative or
  4 25 senator in the general assembly, governor, lieutenant governor,
  4 26 secretary of state, auditor of state, treasurer of state,
  4 27 attorney general, and any other elected state executive
  4 28 officer.  The amendment provides that a member of the house
  4 29 of representatives shall not serve more than six consecutive
  4 30 terms as a representative, and that a member of the senate
  4 31 shall not serve more than three consecutive terms as a senator.
  4 32 The amendment provides that a person elected as governor,
  4 33 lieutenant governor, secretary of state, auditor of state,
  4 34 treasurer of state, or attorney general shall not serve more
  4 35 than three consecutive terms in that respective office. The
  5  1 amendment also provides that if the general assembly provides
  5  2 for the election of a state executive officer, that the officer
  5  3 shall not serve more than 12 consecutive years in that office.
  5  4    The amendment provides that if a person is elected,
  5  5 elevated, or appointed as applicable, to serve a portion of
  5  6 a term in these respective offices, the term shall not be
  5  7 included in counting terms of service if the person did not
  5  8 serve at least one=half of the full term. The amendment
  5  9 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 10 2021.
  5 11    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  5 12 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  5 13 electorate for ratification.

  3  8 elected, but that person died in office or resigned from office
  3  9 or was otherwise removed from office, that portion of a term
  3 10 served shall not be included in the terms of service for
  3 11 purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for at
  3 12 least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on terms
  3 13 of service applies to terms of office beginning on or after
  3 14 January 1, 2021.
  3 15    5.  The Constitution of the State of Iowa is amended by
  3 16 adding the following new section to Article IV:
  3 17 Elected state executive officer ==== term limits.SEC. 23.  If
  3 18 the general assembly provides by law for the election of a
  3 19 state executive officer by the people, a person shall not be
  3 20 elected for a term to that office if the term would result in
  3 21 the person serving more than a total of twelve years in that
  3 22 office. If a person appointed to serve a portion of a term to
  3 23 which some other person was elected, but that person died in
  3 24 office or resigned from office or was otherwise removed from
  3 25 office, that portion of a term served shall not be included
  3 26 in the terms of service for purposes of this limitation if
  3 27 the person did not serve for at least one=half of the term of
  3 28 office. This limitation on terms of service applies to terms
  3 29 of office beginning on or after January 1, 2021.
  3 30    6.  Section 12 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  3 31 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  3 32 Attorney general.SEC. 12.  The general assembly shall
  3 33 provide, by law, for the election of an attorney general by the
  3 34 people, whose term of office shall be four years, and until his
  3 35 successor is elected and qualifies.
  4  1 A person shall not be elected for a term as attorney general
  4  2 if the term would result in the person serving more than a
  4  3 total of three consecutive terms in that office. If a person
  4  4 appointed to serve a portion of a term to which some other
  4  5 person was elected, but that person died in office or resigned
  4  6 from office or was otherwise removed from office, that portion
  4  7 of a term served shall not be included in the terms of service
  4  8 for purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for
  4  9 at least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on
  4 10 terms of service applies to terms of office beginning on or
  4 11 after January 1, 2021.
  4 12    Sec. 2.  REFERRAL AND PUBLICATION.  The foregoing amendment
  4 13 to the Constitution of the State of Iowa is referred to the
  4 14 general assembly to be chosen at the next general election
  4 15 for members of the general assembly, and the secretary of
  4 16 state is directed to cause the same to be published for three
  4 17 consecutive months previous to the date of that election as
  4 18 provided by law.
  4 19                           EXPLANATION
  4 20 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  4 21 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  4 22    This joint resolution proposes an amendment to the
  4 23 Constitution of the State of Iowa limiting terms of service
  4 24 for persons elected to the offices of representative or
  4 25 senator in the general assembly, governor, lieutenant governor,
  4 26 secretary of state, auditor of state, treasurer of state,
  4 27 attorney general, and any other elected state executive
  4 28 officer.  The amendment provides that a member of the house
  4 29 of representatives shall not serve more than six consecutive
  4 30 terms as a representative, and that a member of the senate
  4 31 shall not serve more than three consecutive terms as a senator.
  4 32 The amendment provides that a person elected as governor,
  4 33 lieutenant governor, secretary of state, auditor of state,
  4 34 treasurer of state, or attorney general shall not serve more
  4 35 than three consecutive terms in that respective office. The
  5  1 amendment also provides that if the general assembly provides
  5  2 for the election of a state executive officer, that the officer
  5  3 shall not serve more than 12 consecutive years in that office.
  5  4    The amendment provides that if a person is elected,
  5  5 elevated, or appointed as applicable, to serve a portion of
  5  6 a term in these respective offices, the term shall not be
  5  7 included in counting terms of service if the person did not
  5  8 serve at least one=half of the full term. The amendment
  5  9 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 10 2021.
  5 11    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  5 12 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  5 13 electorate for ratification.

  3  8 elected, but that person died in office or resigned from office
  3  9 or was otherwise removed from office, that portion of a term
  3 10 served shall not be included in the terms of service for
  3 11 purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for at

  3 30    6.  Section 12 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  3 31 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  3 32 Attorney general.SEC. 12.  The general assembly shall
  3 33 provide, by law, for the election of an attorney general by the
  3 34 people, whose term of office shall be four years, and until his
  3 35 successor is elected and qualifies.
  4  1 A person shall not be elected for a term as attorney general
  4  2 if the term would result in the person serving more than a
  4  3 total of three consecutive terms in that office. If a person
  4  4 appointed to serve a portion of a term to which some other
  4  5 person was elected, but that person died in office or resigned
  4  6 from office or was otherwise removed from office, that portion
  4  7 of a term served shall not be included in the terms of service
  4  8 for purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for
  4  9 at least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on
  4 10 terms of service applies to terms of office beginning on or
  4 11 after January 1, 2021.
  4 12    Sec. 2.  REFERRAL AND PUBLICATION.  The foregoing amendment
  4 13 to the Constitution of the State of Iowa is referred to the
  4 14 general assembly to be chosen at the next general election
  4 15 for members of the general assembly, and the secretary of
  4 16 state is directed to cause the same to be published for three
  4 17 consecutive months previous to the date of that election as
  4 18 provided by law.
  4 19                           EXPLANATION
  4 20 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  4 21 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  4 22    This joint resolution proposes an amendment to the
  4 23 Constitution of the State of Iowa limiting terms of service
  4 24 for persons elected to the offices of representative or
  4 25 senator in the general assembly, governor, lieutenant governor,
  4 26 secretary of state, auditor of state, treasurer of state,
  4 27 attorney general, and any other elected state executive
  4 28 officer.  The amendment provides that a member of the house
  4 29 of representatives shall not serve more than six consecutive
  4 30 terms as a representative, and that a member of the senate
  4 31 shall not serve more than three consecutive terms as a senator.
  4 32 The amendment provides that a person elected as governor,
  4 33 lieutenant governor, secretary of state, auditor of state,
  4 34 treasurer of state, or attorney general shall not serve more
  4 35 than three consecutive terms in that respective office. The
  5  1 amendment also provides that if the general assembly provides
  5  2 for the election of a state executive officer, that the officer
  5  3 shall not serve more than 12 consecutive years in that office.
  5  4    The amendment provides that if a person is elected,
  5  5 elevated, or appointed as applicable, to serve a portion of
  5  6 a term in these respective offices, the term shall not be
  5  7 included in counting terms of service if the person did not
  5  8 serve at least one=half of the full term. The amendment
  5  9 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 10 2021.
  5 11    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  5 12 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  5 13 electorate for ratification.

  3 11 purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for at
  3 12 least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on terms

  3 14 January 1, 2021.

  3 22 office. If a person appointed to serve a portion of a term to
  3 23 which some other person was elected, but that person died in
  3 24 office or resigned from office or was otherwise removed from
  3 25 office, that portion of a term served shall not be included
  3 26 in the terms of service for purposes of this limitation if
  3 27 the person did not serve for at least one=half of the term of
  3 28 office. This limitation on terms of service applies to terms
  3 29 of office beginning on or after January 1, 2021.
  3 30    6.  Section 12 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  3 31 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  3 32 Attorney general.SEC. 12.  The general assembly shall
  3 33 provide, by law, for the election of an attorney general by the
  3 34 people, whose term of office shall be four years, and until his
  3 35 successor is elected and qualifies.
  4  1 A person shall not be elected for a term as attorney general
  4  2 if the term would result in the person serving more than a
  4  3 total of three consecutive terms in that office. If a person
  4  4 appointed to serve a portion of a term to which some other
  4  5 person was elected, but that person died in office or resigned
  4  6 from office or was otherwise removed from office, that portion
  4  7 of a term served shall not be included in the terms of service
  4  8 for purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for
  4  9 at least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on
  4 10 terms of service applies to terms of office beginning on or
  4 11 after January 1, 2021.
  4 12    Sec. 2.  REFERRAL AND PUBLICATION.  The foregoing amendment
  4 13 to the Constitution of the State of Iowa is referred to the
  4 14 general assembly to be chosen at the next general election
  4 15 for members of the general assembly, and the secretary of
  4 16 state is directed to cause the same to be published for three
  4 17 consecutive months previous to the date of that election as
  4 18 provided by law.
  4 19                           EXPLANATION
  4 20 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  4 21 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  4 22    This joint resolution proposes an amendment to the
  4 23 Constitution of the State of Iowa limiting terms of service
  4 24 for persons elected to the offices of representative or
  4 25 senator in the general assembly, governor, lieutenant governor,
  4 26 secretary of state, auditor of state, treasurer of state,
  4 27 attorney general, and any other elected state executive
  4 28 officer.  The amendment provides that a member of the house
  4 29 of representatives shall not serve more than six consecutive
  4 30 terms as a representative, and that a member of the senate
  4 31 shall not serve more than three consecutive terms as a senator.
  4 32 The amendment provides that a person elected as governor,
  4 33 lieutenant governor, secretary of state, auditor of state,
  4 34 treasurer of state, or attorney general shall not serve more
  4 35 than three consecutive terms in that respective office. The
  5  1 amendment also provides that if the general assembly provides
  5  2 for the election of a state executive officer, that the officer
  5  3 shall not serve more than 12 consecutive years in that office.
  5  4    The amendment provides that if a person is elected,
  5  5 elevated, or appointed as applicable, to serve a portion of
  5  6 a term in these respective offices, the term shall not be
  5  7 included in counting terms of service if the person did not
  5  8 serve at least one=half of the full term. The amendment
  5  9 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 10 2021.
  5 11    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  5 12 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  5 13 electorate for ratification.

  4 28 officer.  The amendment provides that a member of the house
  4 29 of representatives shall not serve more than six consecutive
  4 30 terms as a representative, and that a member of the senate
  4 31 shall not serve more than three consecutive terms as a senator.
  4 32 The amendment provides that a person elected as governor,
  4 33 lieutenant governor, secretary of state, auditor of state,
  4 34 treasurer of state, or attorney general shall not serve more
  4 35 than three consecutive terms in that respective office. The
  5  1 amendment also provides that if the general assembly provides
  5  2 for the election of a state executive officer, that the officer
  5  3 shall not serve more than 12 consecutive years in that office.
  5  4    The amendment provides that if a person is elected,
  5  5 elevated, or appointed as applicable, to serve a portion of
  5  6 a term in these respective offices, the term shall not be
  5  7 included in counting terms of service if the person did not
  5  8 serve at least one=half of the full term. The amendment
  5  9 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 10 2021.
  5 11    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  5 12 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  5 13 electorate for ratification.
       LSB 5488XS (3) 86
       aw/sc
  3 24 office or resigned from office or was otherwise removed from
  3 25 office, that portion of a term served shall not be included
  3 26 in the terms of service for purposes of this limitation if
  3 27 the person did not serve for at least one=half of the term of
  3 28 office. This limitation on terms of service applies to terms
  3 29 of office beginning on or after January 1, 2021.
  3 30    6.  Section 12 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  3 31 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  3 32 Attorney general.SEC. 12.  The general assembly shall
  3 33 provide, by law, for the election of an attorney general by the
  3 34 people, whose term of office shall be four years, and until his
  3 35 successor is elected and qualifies.
  4  1 A person shall not be elected for a term as attorney general
  4  2 if the term would result in the person serving more than a
  4  3 total of three consecutive terms in that office. If a person
  4  4 appointed to serve a portion of a term to which some other
  4  5 person was elected, but that person died in office or resigned
  4  6 from office or was otherwise removed from office, that portion
  4  7 of a term served shall not be included in the terms of service
  4  8 for purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for
  4  9 at least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on
  4 10 terms of service applies to terms of office beginning on or
  4 11 after January 1, 2021.
  4 12    Sec. 2.  REFERRAL AND PUBLICATION.  The foregoing amendment
  4 13 to the Constitution of the State of Iowa is referred to the
  4 14 general assembly to be chosen at the next general election
  4 15 for members of the general assembly, and the secretary of
  4 16 state is directed to cause the same to be published for three
  4 17 consecutive months previous to the date of that election as
  4 18 provided by law.

  4 14 general assembly to be chosen at the next general election
  4 15 for members of the general assembly, and the secretary of
  4 16 state is directed to cause the same to be published for three
  4 17 consecutive months previous to the date of that election as
  4 18 provided by law.
  4 19                           EXPLANATION
  4 20 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  4 21 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  4 22    This joint resolution proposes an amendment to the
  4 23 Constitution of the State of Iowa limiting terms of service
  4 24 for persons elected to the offices of representative or
  4 25 senator in the general assembly, governor, lieutenant governor,
  4 26 secretary of state, auditor of state, treasurer of state,
  4 27 attorney general, and any other elected state executive
  4 28 officer.  The amendment provides that a member of the house
  4 29 of representatives shall not serve more than six consecutive
  4 30 terms as a representative, and that a member of the senate
  4 31 shall not serve more than three consecutive terms as a senator.
  4 32 The amendment provides that a person elected as governor,
  4 33 lieutenant governor, secretary of state, auditor of state,
  4 34 treasurer of state, or attorney general shall not serve more
  4 35 than three consecutive terms in that respective office. The
  5  1 amendment also provides that if the general assembly provides
  5  2 for the election of a state executive officer, that the officer
  5  3 shall not serve more than 12 consecutive years in that office.
  5  4    The amendment provides that if a person is elected,
  5  5 elevated, or appointed as applicable, to serve a portion of
  5  6 a term in these respective offices, the term shall not be
  5  7 included in counting terms of service if the person did not
  5  8 serve at least one=half of the full term. The amendment
  5  9 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 10 2021.
  5 11    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  5 12 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  5 13 electorate for ratification.
       LSB 5488XS (3) 86
       aw/sc
  3 33 provide, by law, for the election of an attorney general by the
  3 34 people, whose term of office shall be four years, and until his
  3 35 successor is elected and qualifies.
  4  1 A person shall not be elected for a term as attorney general
  4  2 if the term would result in the person serving more than a
  4  3 total of three consecutive terms in that office. If a person
  4  4 appointed to serve a portion of a term to which some other
  4  5 person was elected, but that person died in office or resigned
  4  6 from office or was otherwise removed from office, that portion
  4  7 of a term served shall not be included in the terms of service
  4  8 for purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for
  4  9 at least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on
  4 10 terms of service applies to terms of office beginning on or
  4 11 after January 1, 2021.

  4  8 for purposes of this limitation if the person did not serve for
  4  9 at least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on
  4 10 terms of service applies to terms of office beginning on or
  4 11 after January 1, 2021.
  4 12    Sec. 2.  REFERRAL AND PUBLICATION.  The foregoing amendment
  4 13 to the Constitution of the State of Iowa is referred to the
  4 14 general assembly to be chosen at the next general election
  4 15 for members of the general assembly, and the secretary of
  4 16 state is directed to cause the same to be published for three
  4 17 consecutive months previous to the date of that election as
  4 18 provided by law.
  4 19                           EXPLANATION
  4 20 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  4 21 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  4 22    This joint resolution proposes an amendment to the
  4 23 Constitution of the State of Iowa limiting terms of service
  4 24 for persons elected to the offices of representative or
  4 25 senator in the general assembly, governor, lieutenant governor,
  4 26 secretary of state, auditor of state, treasurer of state,
  4 27 attorney general, and any other elected state executive
  4 28 officer.  The amendment provides that a member of the house
  4 29 of representatives shall not serve more than six consecutive
  4 30 terms as a representative, and that a member of the senate
  4 31 shall not serve more than three consecutive terms as a senator.
  4 32 The amendment provides that a person elected as governor,
  4 33 lieutenant governor, secretary of state, auditor of state,
  4 34 treasurer of state, or attorney general shall not serve more
  4 35 than three consecutive terms in that respective office. The
  5  1 amendment also provides that if the general assembly provides
  5  2 for the election of a state executive officer, that the officer
  5  3 shall not serve more than 12 consecutive years in that office.
  5  4    The amendment provides that if a person is elected,
  5  5 elevated, or appointed as applicable, to serve a portion of
  5  6 a term in these respective offices, the term shall not be
  5  7 included in counting terms of service if the person did not
  5  8 serve at least one=half of the full term. The amendment
  5  9 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 10 2021.
  5 11    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  5 12 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  5 13 electorate for ratification.
       LSB 5488XS (3) 86
       aw/sc
  4  9 at least one=half of the four=year term. This limitation on
  4 10 terms of service applies to terms of office beginning on or
  4 11 after January 1, 2021.

  5  7 included in counting terms of service if the person did not
  5  8 serve at least one=half of the full term. The amendment
  5  9 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 10 2021.
  5 11    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  5 12 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  5 13 electorate for ratification.
       LSB 5488XS (3) 86
       aw/sc
  4 23 Constitution of the State of Iowa limiting terms of service
  4 24 for persons elected to the offices of representative or
  4 25 senator in the general assembly, governor, lieutenant governor,
  4 26 secretary of state, auditor of state, treasurer of state,
  4 27 attorney general, and any other elected state executive
  4 28 officer.  The amendment provides that a member of the house
  4 29 of representatives shall not serve more than six consecutive
  4 30 terms as a representative, and that a member of the senate
  4 31 shall not serve more than three consecutive terms as a senator.
  4 32 The amendment provides that a person elected as governor,
  4 33 lieutenant governor, secretary of state, auditor of state,
  4 34 treasurer of state, or attorney general shall not serve more
  4 35 than three consecutive terms in that respective office. The
  5  1 amendment also provides that if the general assembly provides
  5  2 for the election of a state executive officer, that the officer
  5  3 shall not serve more than 12 consecutive years in that office.
  5  4    The amendment provides that if a person is elected,
  5  5 elevated, or appointed as applicable, to serve a portion of
  5  6 a term in these respective offices, the term shall not be
  5  7 included in counting terms of service if the person did not
  5  8 serve at least one=half of the full term. The amendment
  5  9 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 10 2021.
  5 11    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  5 12 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  5 13 electorate for ratification.
       LSB 5488XS (3) 86
